posted:Posted October 14, 2021
msg:Every time I travel to Guilin in recent years, I basically choose this hotel. Although it is not an international brand chain, it is a local five-star hotel with good hardware and services and a high cost performance.

The room is spacious and the bedding is comfortable. The service at the front desk was good. It is estimated that I forgot this time. The welcome fruit was not prepared in advance, and the phone in the room could not be dialed. Affect the check-in experience, compared with the previous few times a bit inferior. Hope it can be optimized in the future.
